Func RUNGTHONGXANH()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf

_RUNGTHONGXANH()  ;Checkpoint 2
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1079883451")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "1079660471")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "3224352214")
	WEnd
